 \"text\": \"The Kubernetes API deprecation policy is enforced through a multi-layered system implemented in kubernetes/kubernetes. The core enforcement mechanisms are:\\n\\n1. **API Version Deprecation Detection and Warning Injection** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/deprecation/deprecation.go):\\n   - The `IsDeprecated()` function checks if an API version is deprecated by comparing the current Kubernetes version against APILifecycleDeprecated() versions implemented in each API type.\\n   - The `RemovedRelease()` function extracts the removal version from objects implementing APILifecycleRemoved().\\n   - The `WarningMessage()` function generates human-readable deprecation warnings that include the version when the API was deprecated, when it will be removed, and suggested replacements.\\n   - The `MajorMinor()` function parses version information for comparison.\\n\\n2. **Removal Version Validation** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/deleted_kinds.go):\\n   - The `ResourceExpirationEvaluator` interface and implementation enforce removal version checks.\\n   - The `ShouldServeForVersion()` method determines whether an API should continue to be served based on its removal version versus the current Kubernetes version.\\n   - The `RemoveDeletedKinds()` method removes storage for API kinds that have reached their removal version, effectively preventing them from being served (with exceptions for alpha releases and emergency override).\\n   - This uses the APILifecycleIntroduced and APILifecycleRemoved interfaces to determine version boundaries.\\n\\n3. **Minimum Supported API Version Validation** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/storage/resource_encoding_config.go):\\n   - Storage version selection logic checks APILifecycleIntroduced() to ensure only API versions that were introduced in or before the current compatibility version are used.\\n   - This prevents using storage versions for API types that didn't exist in earlier compatibility versions.\\n\\n4. **Warning Injection into Responses** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/installer.go):\\n   - During endpoint registration in `registerResourceHandlers()`, deprecated APIs are identified and their deprecation status is tracked.\\n   - The `deprecation.IsDeprecated()` function is called with the current Kubernetes version to determine deprecation status.\\n   - Warnings are generated via `deprecation.WarningMessage()` and injected into responses.\\n\\n5. **Warning Recording and Deduplication** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/warning/warning.go and staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/warning.go):\\n   - The `AddWarningsHandler()` function in warning.go adds warnings to request contexts.\\n   - The `WithWarningRecorder()` filter in filters/warning.go manages warning deduplication and size limits (4KB total, 256 runes per warning) to ensure responses remain valid.\\n   - Warnings are sent as HTTP Warning headers (RFC 7234 code 299) in API responses.\\n\\n6. **Metrics and Audit Logging** (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/metrics/metrics.go):\\n   - The `deprecatedRequestGauge` metric tracks requests to deprecated APIs by group, version, resource, subresource, and removed_release version.\\n   - The `MonitorRequest()` function records deprecated API usage.\\n   - The `InstrumentRouteFunc()` wraps route handlers to capture deprecation information.\\n   - Audit annotations are added with the removed_release version for compliance tracking.\\n\\n7. **API Installation and Enforcement** (pkg/controlplane/apiserver/apis.go):\\n   - The `InstallAPIs()` method creates a `ResourceExpirationEvaluator` based on the current Kubernetes version.\\n   - It calls `RemoveDeletedKinds()` on each API group to remove storage for APIs whose removal version has been reached.\\n   - This prevents the API server from serving API versions that are no longer supported.\\n\\nThese files work together to implement the complete API deprecation policy: detecting deprecated API versions, warning users about their use, preventing removed API versions from being served, and recording telemetry for deprecation enforcement.
